# Focus Schools & Operator Upgrades

# Nightwave
Nightwave challenge tiers, challenge types, and reward pool. Includes weekly, daily, and elite challenges with their standing values.
**Affiliation:** RadioLegionIntermission15Syndicate

## Challenges
### Glider
Kill |COUNT| Enemies while Aim Gliding
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 15

### Trampoline
Bullet Jump |COUNT| times.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Researcher
Scan |COUNT| Objects or Enemies.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 15

### Saver
Pick up |COUNT| Credits.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 15000

### Agent
Complete a Mission.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 1

### Graffiti
Deploy a Glyph while on a mission.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 1

### Warning Shot
Kill |COUNT| Enemies.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 200

### Power Trip
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Abilities.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Detonator
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Blast Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Meltdown
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Corrosive Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Short Circuit
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Electricity Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Executioner
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Finishers.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 10

### Arsonist
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Heat Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Deep Freeze
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Cold Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Biohazard
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Gas Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Marksman
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Headshots.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 40

### Attractive
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Magnetic Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Sword Dance
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with a Melee Weapon.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Poisoner
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Toxin Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Mow Them Down
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with a Primary Weapon.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Reactor
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Radiation Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Smaller is Bigger
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with a Secondary Weapon.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Go Viral
Kill |COUNT| Enemies with Viral Damage.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 150

### Energizing
Pick up |COUNT| Energy Orbs.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 20

### Shiny
Pick up |COUNT| Mods.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 8

### Communicator
Mark |COUNT| Mods or Resources.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 5

### Expressive
Play |COUNT| Emote.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 1

### Accelerator
Kill |COUNT| Enemies while Sliding.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 10

### Thrill Rider
Kill |COUNT| enemies while riding a K-Drive, Kaithe, Velocipod, or Atomicycle.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 20

### Liquidation
Sell any item in your Inventory for Credits.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 1

### Two for One
Pierce and kill 2 or more enemies in a single Bow shot.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 1

### Swatter
Kill |COUNT| Drones or Ospreys with your Melee Weapon.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 3

### Topping Off the Tank
Successfully defend an Excavator without allowing it to run out of power.
**Standing:** 1000 | **Required:** 1

### The Personal Touch
Place 1 decoration in your Orbiter.

# Public Export — Syndicates (Detailed)
Full syndicate data from the official export including rank titles, standing requirements, initiation sacrifices, and offerings at each rank.

## Arbiters of Hexis
The dogmatic Arbiters seek a truth through discipline and practice. They reject the Tenno as Warrior mythology... A lie constructed to limit their potential.

### Ranks
| Rank | Title | Standing |
|---|---|---|
| 5 | Maxim | 240000 |
| 4 | Crusader | 141000 |
| 3 | Lawful | 71000 |
| 2 | Authentic | 27000 |
| 1 | Principled | 5000 |
| -1 | Deceiver | -27000 |
| -2 | Fraud | -71000 |
**Initiation Cost:** 500 AlloyPlate

## Cephalon Suda
A vast consciousness watching with a curious eye. Seemingly devoid of emotion, Suda's thirst for knowledge and abhorrence of destruction can only be described as passionate.

### Ranks
| Rank | Title | Standing |
|---|---|---|
| 5 | Genius | 240000 |
| 4 | Wise | 141000 |
| 3 | Intelligent | 71000 |
| 2 | Intriguing | 27000 |
| 1 | Competent | 5000 |
| -1 | Debris | -27000 |
| -2 | Waste | -71000 |
**Initiation Cost:** 500 Circuits

## Conclave
A warrior only grows if they face the ultimate enemy. Themselves.

### Ranks
| Rank | Title | Standing |
|---|---|---|
| 5 | Typhoon | 240000 |
| 4 | Hurricane | 141000 |
| 3 | Tempest | 71000 |
| 2 | Whirlwind | 27000 |
| 1 | Mistral | 5000 |
**Initiation Cost:** 100 Plastids

## Entrati
Heirs to the legacy of Albrecht Entrati, his powerful Orokin family encountered disaster, isolation and bitter division on Deimos. The arrival of the Tenno, beneficiaries of their Void research, may bring fresh hope - and a deeper understanding of the world that has trapped their family.

### Ranks
| Rank | Title | Standing |
|---|---|---|
| 5 | FAMILY | 240000 |
| 4 | FRIEND | 141000 |
| 3 | ASSOCIATE | 71000 |
| 2 | ACQUAINTANCE | 27000 |
| 1 | STRANGER | 5000 |

## Necraloid
While the Entrati family's cohort of lethal Necramechs succumbed to the corrupting influence of Deimos, Loid's shielding kept him sane, as well as preserving what was left of his 'passenger', the Cephalon Otak. Together they maintain a proud tradition of loyal service.

### Ranks
| Rank | Title | Standing |
|---|---|---|
| 3 | CLEARANCE: ODIMA | 71000 |
| 2 | CLEARANCE: MODUS | 27000 |
| 1 | CLEARANCE: AGNESIS | 5000 |

## Cavia
Animals sent into the Void by Albrecht Entrati, the three surviving Cavia came back changed forever. They gained human intelligence, but could speak only incoherent Voidtongue until the Jahu Gargoyle made them intelligible. Despite what Albrecht did to them, they have resolved to assist his chosen Operator.

### Ranks
| Rank | Title | Standing |
|---|---|---|
| 5 | Illuminate | 240000 |
| 4 | Scholar | 141000 |
| 3 | Colleague | 71000 |
| 2 | Researcher | 27000 |
| 1 | Assistant | 5000 |

## Operational Supply
Support and rewards for Tenno fighting in active operations.

### Ranks
| Rank | Title | Standing |
|---|---|---|
| 3 | CHAMPION | 6000 |
| 2 | DEFENDER | 3000 |
| 1 | COLLABORATOR | 1000 |

## The Hex
Formerly human operatives, the six members of the Hex were transformed into Protoframes by Albrecht Entrati. Filled with uncanny power and mourning their lost humanity, they continue their mission of mercy in beleaguered Höllvania.

### Ranks
| Rank | Title | Standing |
|---|---|---|
| 5 | Pizza Party | 240000 |
| 4 | Hot & Fresh | 141000 |
| 3 | 2-for-1 | 71000 |
| 2 | Fresh Slice | 27000 |
| 1 | Leftovers | 5000 |

## Cephalon Simaris
Through Synthesis we can rebuild and preserve. Create memory-immortals within this data oasis. Will you become enlightened, Tenno? Will you hunt for me?

## New Loka
Only through the restoration of a pure humanity and the repopulation of Earth can the conflict end. The New Loka are worshipers of the human form and Earth, before its corruption.

A tight knit band of merchants, hucksters, and survivors, the Ostrons call Cetus their home. The town was built around an Orokin Tower, that both protects and nourishes them.

## Red Veil
The Veil see corruption all around them. They are honor-bound to heal the system through a great and violent purge. No cost too great, no blood too precious.

## Solaris United
Risen from the ashes, Solaris United returns to free the Solaris people from their mental shackles and physical servitude. No being should have to work to own their own mind, their own body, their own future.

## Ventkids
Hangin' with their logical fam in the ducts of Fortuna, the Ventkids get by stealing parts from the Corpus and running K-Drive races out on the Vallis. At night the ventways bang to the sound of skeg - to the chagrin of the locals.
